        const hamburger = document.getElementById('hamburger');
        const mobileMenu = document.getElementById('mobileMenu');

        hamburger.addEventListener('click', function() {
            mobileMenu.classList.toggle('active');
        });

        function toggleMobileDropdown(button) {
            const dropdown = button.nextElementSibling;
            dropdown.classList.toggle('open');
            button.querySelector('.chevron').classList.toggle('rotate');
        }
    </script>

    <script>
        // OPTIMIZATION: Critical path - minimal blocking code
        function setupHero() {
            // Lazy load tools database
            function getToolsDatabase() {
                return [
                    { name: 'PDF Converter', category: 'pdf' },
                    { name: 'Image Editor', category: 'image' },
                    { name: 'Video Compressor', category: 'video' },
                    { name: 'AI Writer', category: 'ai' },
                    { name: 'Web Inspector', category: 'web' },
                    { name: 'Text Formatter', category: 'text' },
                    { name: 'QR Code Generator', category: 'qr' },
                    { name: 'PDF Splitter', category: 'pdf' },
                    { name: 'Image Resizer', category: 'image' },
                    { name: 'Video Editor', category: 'video' },
                    { name: 'AI Translator', category: 'ai' },
                    { name: 'HTML to PDF', category: 'web' }
                ];
            }

            // Passive event listeners (no blocking)
            document.querySelectorAll('.category-btn').forEach(btn => {
                btn.addEventListener('click', function() {
                    const category = this.dataset.category;
                    const toolsDatabase = getToolsDatabase();
                    const filtered = toolsDatabase.filter(t => t.category === category);
                    console.log(`${filtered.length} tools in ${category.toUpperCase()}`);
                }, { passive: true });
            });
        }

        // OPTIMIZATION: Use requestIdleCallback for non-critical tasks
        if ('requestIdleCallback' in window) {
            requestIdleCallback(setupHero, { timeout: 2000 });
        } else {
            // Fallback for older browsers
            setTimeout(setupHero, 0);
        }

        // OPTIMIZATION: Canvas animation only after page fully loaded
        window.addEventListener('load', function() {
            const canvas = document.getElementById('particleCanvas');
            if (!canvas) return;
            
            const isMobile = window.innerWidth <= 768;
            
            if (isMobile) {
                canvas.remove();
            } else {
                // Load after full page render (3s max)
                if ('requestIdleCallback' in window) {
                    requestIdleCallback(() => initializeParticles(), { timeout: 3000 });
                } else {
                    setTimeout(initializeParticles, 2500);
                }
            }
        }, { passive: true });

        // Cleanup
        window.addEventListener('beforeunload', function() {
            document.querySelectorAll('.category-btn').forEach(btn => {
                btn.removeEventListener('click', arguments.callee);
            });
        });
    </script>

    <!-- OPTIMIZATION: Defer non-critical script loading -->
    <script defer>
        // Preload particles only on high-speed connections
        if (navigator.connection && navigator.connection.saveData === false) {
            // Optional future optimization
        }
    </script>

<script>
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
  // Get all filter categories and tools block results
  const filterCategories = document.querySelectorAll('.filter__category');
  const toolsBlocks = document.querySelectorAll('.tools-block-results');

  // Function to reset active class on all categories
  const resetActiveClass = () => {
    filterCategories.forEach(category => category.classList.remove('is-active'));
  };

  // Add click event listener to each filter category
  filterCategories.forEach(category => {
    category.addEventListener('click', () => {
      // Get the data-tools-block-type of the clicked category
      const blockType = category.getAttribute('data-tools-block-type');

      // Reset active class and set it for the clicked category
      resetActiveClass();
      category.classList.add('is-active');

      // Show/hide the corresponding tools block
      toolsBlocks.forEach(block => {
        if (blockType === 'all' || block.getAttribute('data-tools-block-type') === blockType) {
          block.style.display = 'flex'; // Display as flex to maintain the grid layout
        } else {
          block.style.display = 'none';
        }
      });
    });
  });
});

</script>

    <script>
        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
            const container = document.getElementById('timelineContainer');
            const progress = document.getElementById('timelineProgress');
            const cards = document.querySelectorAll('.milestone-card');

            function updateTimeline() {
                if (!container || !progress) return;

                const rect = container.getBoundingClientRect();
                const windowHeight = window.innerHeight;
                const containerHeight = container.offsetHeight;

                // Update progress line
                const scrollProgress = Math.max(0, Math.min(1, (windowHeight - rect.top) / (windowHeight + containerHeight)));
                progress.style.height = (scrollProgress * 100) + '%';

                // Show cards on scroll
                const triggerPoint = windowHeight * 0.75;
                cards.forEach((card) => {
                    const cardRect = card.getBoundingClientRect();
                    if (cardRect.top < triggerPoint) {
                        card.classList.add('visible');
                    }
                });
            }

            window.addEventListener('scroll', updateTimeline);
            window.addEventListener('resize', updateTimeline);
            
            // Initial check
            setTimeout(updateTimeline, 100);
        });
    </script>

    <script>
        function toggleFAQ(button, index) {
            const answer = document.getElementById('answer-' + index);
            const chevron = button.querySelector('.faq-chevron');
            
            document.querySelectorAll('.faq-answer').forEach((ans, i) => {
                if (i !== index) {
                    ans.classList.remove('active');
                    document.querySelectorAll('.faq-button')[i].querySelector('.faq-chevron').classList.remove('rotated');
                }
            });

            answer.classList.toggle('active');
            chevron.classList.toggle('rotated');
        }

        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
            // All items start collapsed
        });
    </script>

<!-- Bait element with ad-related ID and class -->
<div id="advertisement-test" class="advertisement ads-banner adsbygoogle" style="height:1px;width:1px;opacity:0;"></div>

<style>
  @keyframes pulse {
    0%,100% { transform:scale(1) rotate(0deg); }
    50% { transform:scale(1.1) rotate(-5deg); }
  }
</style>

<script>
  (function() {
    setTimeout(function() {
      var elem = document.getElementById('advertisement-test');
      var popup = document.getElementById('adBlockerPopup');
      
      if (!elem) {
        // Element removed by ad blocker
        popup.style.display = 'flex';
      } else {
        var rect = elem.getBoundingClientRect();
        var style = window.getComputedStyle(elem);
        
        // Check if ad blocker is hiding element via CSS
        if (style.display === 'none' || 
            style.visibility === 'hidden' || 
            elem.offsetParent === null ||
            (rect.width === 0 && rect.height === 0 && style.opacity === '0' && style.pointerEvents === 'none')) {
          
          popup.style.display = 'flex';
        } else {
          popup.style.display = 'none';
        }
      }
    }, 2000);
  })();
</script>
